  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2a4b0d51-3b61-4b63-85cd-77d7f138bcf7'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

Her impossibly gorgeous best friend, Zayne, is forever off-limits thanks to the mysterious powers of her soul-stealing kiss. The Warden clan that has always protected her is suddenly keeping dangerous secrets. And she can barely think about Roth, the wickedly hot demon prince who understood her in ways no one else could.<br /><br />But sometimes rock bottom is only the beginning. Because suddenly Layla’s powers begin to evolve, and she’s offered a tantalizing taste of what has always been forbidden. Then, when she least expects it, Roth returns, bringing news that could change her world forever. This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    To me Zayne has a lot of pull in his Warden coven and should have been championing for Layla and getting people to understand her and help make her fe<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    To me Zayne has a lot of pull in his Warden coven and should have been championing for Layla and getting people to understand her and help make her feel more comfortable, but he did nothing other than a small handful of times and if daddy said so then it was so. She would also never feel comfortable being 100% herself around him. I think Zayne is a decent person and great guy... just not what Layla needs.<br /><a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>

<div id="review_554794115" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/554794115" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/554794115?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=1-2-stars-read">1-2-stars-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer554794115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14064674954558299241">My Roth, Layla and Zayne:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416485518i/11975977._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have always been a fan of paranormal YA stories by Jennifer L. Armentrout. Why such a low rating this time? I had to take one star down because of cheesy dialogues and writing style. Second star was taken down because of stereotypical characters and dragged out plotline. And another stars was taken down because of the worst case of love triangle ever. Let me explain.<br/><br/><u>- Cheesy dialogues and writing style -</u><br/><br/>Cheesy according to Urban Dictionary: <i>"Trying too hard, unsubtle, </i></span>
  <span id="freeText14064674954558299241" style="display:none">My Roth, Layla and Zayne:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416485518i/11975977._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have always been a fan of paranormal YA stories by Jennifer L. Armentrout. Why such a low rating this time? I had to take one star down because of cheesy dialogues and writing style. Second star was taken down because of stereotypical characters and dragged out plotline. And another stars was taken down because of the worst case of love triangle ever. Let me explain.<br><br><u>- Cheesy dialogues and writing style -</u><br><br>Cheesy according to Urban Dictionary: <i>"Trying too hard, unsubtle, and inauthentic. Specifically that which is unsubtle or inauthentic in its way of trying to elicit a certain response from a viewer, listener, audience, etc."</i> This is exactly what Mrs. Armentrout achieved in this book. I guess she was aiming for sounding young and cool. However, phrases and dialogues she presented felt foolish and over the top. Constant use of phrases like <i>"holy granola bar"</i>, <i>"crap on a cracker"</i>, <i>"Christ on a crutch"</i>, <i>"thank baby Jesus and cuddly angels"</i> or <i>"holly shit balls for Sunday dinner"</i> annoyed me big time and made characters look rather immature in my opinion. I am sure many readers won't be bothered by it, but it didn't work for me at all.<br><br><u>- Stereotypical characters and dragged out plotline -</u><br><br>Mrs. Armentrout presented nothing new in this book. We have seen it all in her previous books or in other books within YA genre. There is nothing special that would distinguish main characters of this series from other YA heroes and heroines. Yes, author came up with some pretty interesting twists towards the end. But even exciting last 20% couldn't change the fact that I was a little bit bored during first 80% of the book.<br><br><u>- The worst case of love triangle -</u><br><br>What was my biggest problem with this love triangle? The fact that Layla acted on her feelings towards both boys. If she was with one boy and internally struggling with her feelings for another boy, I could survive that (sort of). But the fact that she was leading both guys on simultaneously, alternatively being with one while thinking of other and vice versa... Who does something like that? A character I can't feel any compassion for. Plus both guys were willing to forgive Layla everything. And I really mean EVERYTHING. Zayne especially. And that is unhealthy. I couldn't respect them because of it and they all lost my sympathies in this book. And when I don't feel for characters, I simply can't enjoy the story.<br><br>So whose team I am on? <b>Team Roth or Team Zayne? TEAM BAMBI!</b><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14064674954558299241" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1091029462" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1091029462" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

  <span id="freeText8615928576075856334" style="display:none">LAYLA, IF YOU DON'T HOLD ROTH DOWN AND HAVE YOUR SEXY, DIRTY, KINKY, AND POSSIBLY ROUGH WAY WITH HIM IN THIS BOOK...I WILL. <br /><br />AND FORGET ZAYNE ALREADY. HE NEEDS TO BE WITH DANIKA. LIKE, NOW.<br /><br />........................<br /><br />Ugh. I feel so so lame for not realising this would mainly be about Zayne from the Title. STONE COLD TOUCH. DUHHHH.<br /><br />I seriously cannot believe the things that happened in this book. Jennifer really is striving to blow minds. There's so much crazy. Crazy good and crazy baaaad. <br /><br />Don't read on if you haven't read the book. Spoilers will be EVERYWHERE. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Okay. Number one major shock is this love triangle, y'all. Wth is going on?! Roth or Zayne, girl?! You cannot play them back and forth. I personally think that Roth is a better match for you, but Zayne was kicking some serious sexiness in this one. The Bambi scene was whoa. Big shock. And then the side of the road makeout session, where wtf! They can kiss! And then that just all falls apart like it was bound to anyway. <br /><br />Abbott is a major asshole, Zayne is so slow to figure that shit out, and Dez you are amazeballs. <br />Had to do a shoutout for him. <br /><br />Zayne and Danika would make a sweet couple. Let's make that happen, YEAH? <br /><br />Layla can rock Bambi all she wants, it wont change the fact that she belongs with Roth. <br /><br />Roth is just a freaking god. Ugh. Jen does this to me with Seth and now Roth. Similar sense of humors, right? And that's all it really takes for me to be sprung. Well, there's more to it but that's the gist. <br /><br />The whole dying scene...gah! I can't believe he said it. <br />He said ily. Wow. <br /><br />And then there's Layla's ever present doubt that she hears such things. Ugh. <br />She's not the greatest, but she's alright. <br /><br />Poor sweet Sam. What the hello kitty, guys!? How did that happen? I kind of suspected something because he was changing so drastically and wasn't saying much. I have no clue how this will all go down in the next book. <br /><br />I hope Layla picks someone. Roth Roth Roth. <br /><br />I hope that she can get Sam back, without making a deal with the Boss to get his soul back. <br /><br />I do know mommy dearest will break free eventually and I'm kind of excited about that. What kind of mayhem will she cause for Layla? Is it weird that I'm suspecting she will hit on Roth? Or maybe Zayne...she does have a thing for wardens, no?<br /><br />And what's the favor for saving Layla's life? I don't know bout those witches, as they're a wee bit ominous.<br /><br />Ugh. I. need. the. next. book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12055892595567494688">Jennifer does it again! Stone Cold Touch is truly a riveting and beautiful read. If I could rate this book 10 stars I would!! </span>

<div id="review_761694607" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/761694607" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/761694607?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761694607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8633107590554004672"><b> 4.75 stars! </b><br/><br/>I FREAKING LOVE JLA!!!<br/><br/><b> Stone Cold Touch </b> continues the series with Layla adjusting to her usual life again without the demon Roth. Pretty soon she and the Wardens discover a Lilin has been born, a powerful demon that can turn humans into wraiths, and it seems to be Layla's fault.<br/><br/>I thought that this was a wonderful middle book to a trilogy. It brought on all of the feels and the angst. Plus Zayne finally got a shot at wooing Layla which I am all for. I root for the underdog about 99.</span>
  <span id="freeText8633107590554004672" style="display:none"><b> 4.75 stars! </b><br><br>I FREAKING LOVE JLA!!!<br><br><b> Stone Cold Touch </b> continues the series with Layla adjusting to her usual life again without the demon Roth. Pretty soon she and the Wardens discover a Lilin has been born, a powerful demon that can turn humans into wraiths, and it seems to be Layla's fault.<br><br>I thought that this was a wonderful middle book to a trilogy. It brought on all of the feels and the angst. Plus Zayne finally got a shot at wooing Layla which I am all for. I root for the underdog about 99.9% of the time, so for this books guys I am a member of Team Zayne. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/zayne.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413959244i/11586551.png" alt=" photo zayne.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>No really, I even voted for him. <br><br>Not to say that I don't love Roth either, I just have a feeling he's going to win the fan vote, so I'm crossing my fingers for the sweet guy who's loved Layla for years. The bad boy is welcome to stick around too.<br><br>I also loved all of the Buffy references, being the ridiculous nerd that I am. I mean, what else would demons/vampires use for poker currency other than kittens?<br><br>Anyways, not my best review but all I have to say is, read this series. It's like book crack for your brain!<br><br><br>(And why not 5 stars? Because she threw in the "Holy Granola Bar" AGAIN. I was really sick of that in her other books Stay With Me and Opposition, so luckily she didn't use these exaggerations too often in this one). <br><br>***Quotes to possibly be added at a later time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8633107590554004672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_867113498" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/867113498" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/867113498?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23437430-stone-cold-touch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=gargoyles">gargoyles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer867113498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12995997444579306899"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/jla2_zps09c8d7d0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867248.jpg' alt=' photo jla2_zps09c8d7d0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Stone Cold Touch is book two in The Dark Elements series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. OH…MY…GOSH!!!!! This book was amazing. I don’t even know where to start except that I loved it! <br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/jla1_zps79ebacf3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867249.jpg' alt=' photo jla1_zps79ebacf3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>Roth has been gone about two weeks and Layla is grieving. She believes Roth to be suffering in the depths of the fiery pits of hell. Roth became important to her. She can’t label her feelings but knows they are deep. And she misses him desperately. So you can understand her surprise when he shows up at the War</span>
  <span id="freeText12995997444579306899" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/jla2_zps09c8d7d0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867248.jpg" alt=" photo jla2_zps09c8d7d0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Stone Cold Touch is book two in The Dark Elements series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. OH…MY…GOSH!!!!! This book was amazing. I don’t even know where to start except that I loved it! <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/jla1_zps79ebacf3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867249.jpg" alt=" photo jla1_zps79ebacf3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Roth has been gone about two weeks and Layla is grieving. She believes Roth to be suffering in the depths of the fiery pits of hell. Roth became important to her. She can’t label her feelings but knows they are deep. And she misses him desperately. So you can understand her surprise when he shows up at the Warden’s compound looking just fine. Roth is back!!!<br><br>About here is where there is so much I want to say but don’t want to spoil anything. I will say that my love for Roth took a blow at this point. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_m1nnbkkN8I1rsddxho1_500_zpsc036fda9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867250.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_m1nnbkkN8I1rsddxho1_500_zpsc036fda9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Layla’s relationship with Zayne began to change about this time. He started spending more and more time with her, touching her, cuddling with her. Layla knew this was dangerous. The part of her that is half demon feeds off of souls and because of this, she can never kiss Zayne. There can’t be a future with him, can there? But Zayne has other thoughts on this subject.<br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s obvious to everyone but you, Zayne wants you. And, he’s in love with you.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_ne0ko5lUEF1thzaofo1_500_zpsmoyzzxjg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415931210ra/11867251.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ne0ko5lUEF1thzaofo1_500_zpsmoyzzxjg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Part of the reason Roth was sent back is to hunt for a demon called the Lilin whom they believe has been killing innocent people and turning their souls into wraiths. But try as they might, they couldn’t find any evidence of whether there was a Lilin or not. Layla’s demon powers have been changing, evolving, getting stronger. Could all the bad events that have taken place have anything to do with her? Could she have caused them? Is she dangerous without even knowing it? <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n9e4yt7dz11thchzko1_1280_zps59ec9439.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867252._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n9e4yt7dz11thchzko1_1280_zps59ec9439.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When Layla is with Zayne, she feels warm, safe, special, comfortable. She spent her life following him around like a puppy dog. Is it possible that all her childhood dreams could possibly come true? Roth, now, is a different story. He challenges her and evokes all sorts of tummy swirls. But he’s a demon. All he could do is hurt her in the end, right?<br><br><b>
  <i>“Roth was like this little devil on my shoulder, urging me to be bad and to enjoy every freaking moment of it. Except he wasn’t a little devil. He was the Crown Prince of Hell.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n1s0sfXYUC1swx43mo1_500_zpsb2zkiddg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415931210ra/11867253.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n1s0sfXYUC1swx43mo1_500_zpsb2zkiddg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At times my heart broke for Layla. I mean, she doesn’t feel like she belongs anywhere. She eats her meals alone or in the kitchen. Never in the dining room with the rest of the family. At school, no one knows what she really is. She is constantly at war with herself, taught that her demon side is evil. But the wardens don’t accept her either. Where does she belong? And her sort of adoptive father, Abbot. I never liked that guy. Yes, he took her in, but he never really showed her any affection or made her feel like she was a part of the family. And in this book, my feelings of dislike turned to feelings of…well, lets just say they are now much stronger than dislike.<br><br>One little insignificant point I want to make is that this takes place right around Thanksgiving so even though it really doesn’t mean anything, I like that I read it when it is almost Thanksgiving. <br><br>And lets talk ending…well ladies and gentlemen, I want to warn you to hold on to your hats because the last 20% or so of this book will cause you great anxiety. Yes, you will freak out. So don’t say I didn’t warn you. And yes, there is a HUGE FREAKING CLIFFHANGER! And the final book doesn’t come out until I think it said the end of July 2015. What a cruel punishment this is, leaving us like this to wait eight months for the grand finale. This is torture.<br><br>So, did I enjoy this book? Well, if I wasn’t clear enough already, YES, I loved it. And am I still team Roth or have I gone over to the Zayne team? Team Roth, baby, all the way!<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/jla_zpsbafd1f90.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867254.jpg" alt=" photo jla_zpsbafd1f90.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="12995997444579306899" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3230956920457486344">My love for Roth has officially been solidified after that ending! Roth reminds me so much of Daemon; he's witty, sexy, sarcastic, and extremely romantic/passionate! #TeamROTH <br/><br/>Also...<br/>-That cliffhanger is going to cause one serious book hangover...where's book three?!?!<br/>-Bambi the snake is awesome-sauce and apparently also a fan of Wardens <br/>-Abbott = boooo<br/>-Loved all the action that went down<br/>-Roth, Roth, and ROTH!!</span>

<div id="review_1372410618" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1372410618" />
    <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34403359"><img alt="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469758679p2/34403359.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1372410618?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" href="/user/show/34403359">☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1372410618" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9948477703417079181">Oh my goodness. For one thing, I just finished that book in one day. In less than six hours. Also, that was a <b> STUNNING BOOK! </b> I have to admit, I wasn't sure how the second book was going to. My breath was blown away with what I encountered in the second, and somewhat better, installment of the Dark Elements.<br/><br/>So this book starts up from the major and upsetting cliffhanger at the end of <i> White Hot Kiss. </i> Layla is still upset about Roth but that makes sense since he only left two weeks prior. What </span>
  <span id="freeText9948477703417079181" style="display:none">Oh my goodness. For one thing, I just finished that book in one day. In less than six hours. Also, that was a <b> STUNNING BOOK! </b> I have to admit, I wasn't sure how the second book was going to. My breath was blown away with what I encountered in the second, and somewhat better, installment of the Dark Elements.<br><br>So this book starts up from the major and upsetting cliffhanger at the end of <i> White Hot Kiss. </i> Layla is still upset about Roth but that makes sense since he only left two weeks prior. What makes it worse if Zayne, her incredibly gorgeous best friend. Who is totally off limits because of who they both are. And because of the fact that Layla can take his soul if they kiss. Along with that, the lack of trust that the other Wardens have for her have her fearing that they are keeping even more, and worse, secrets. To top it off, there are mystery accidents going on in the school. Overall Layla thinks that nothing could make this worse. But alas, it does.<br><br>Layla's powers begin changing and she gets the chance to see what she has been missing, which leads to a very steamy car scene. Those of you who've read the book, know what I mean.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440445007ra/15976158.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>On top of that Roth returns. At that point, Layla (and I) think that everything is going to be alright. But again alas, its not. Layla has her heart ripped out again as things continue to spiral downward and the death count continuing to rise.<br><br>So now it's time to describe what I like.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432320966ra/14933427.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That about sums it up but I'll continue to try anyway.<br><br>The love...shape. It wasn't exactly a love triangle but I don't know how else to describe it.<br><br><i> “I love you Layla. Do you hear me? I've loved you since the first moment I heard your voice and I will continue to love you. No matter what. I love you.” </i><br><br><i>“I’d find myself unable to stop staring at you, and it was hard not wanting to spend time with you. Why else did I always get up so early?...Can’t think about you? Can’t tell you that you have always been the most amazing girl I’ve ever known? That I can’t hold you? Touch you? Because the last time I checked, I could do all those things.” </i><br><br>Layla. She was an amazing lead girl. I thought that she might be a little weak from the first one but she was very strong in this one. All of my doubts about her just threw out the window.<br><br>Roth. I was laughing at half of the things he was crying and crying at the other. I was heartbroken and crying with Layla because I was rootin' for him since the first book.<br><br>Zayne. I was growing to love him too but I was still a little reluctant to fully accept him. He is a great character and I want to read more with him.<br><br>The action was very good. There was always twists and turns that I didn't see coming. I really loved that there was not one problem throughout the book. There were layers. Like an onion.<br><br>The ending. I knew that there was something wrong with him! No one listened to me! Didn't they hear my internal screaming?! I guess not. No, I wasn't expecting it to be that bad but I knew that there was something a little off with you-know-who that doesn't just have to do with confidence.<br><br>So, there wasn't a thing that I didn't like in this book and it was amazing.<br><br>You should read it because:<br><br><b> 1. The reasons I just listed<br><br>2. Jennifer Armentrout wrote it </b> do you need a better reason than that? I don't think so.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9948477703417079181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_750264286" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/750264286" />
    <a title="Patricia Huynh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21807988-patricia-huynh"><img alt="Patricia Huynh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577282096p2/21807988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/750264286?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patricia Huynh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patricia Huynh" href="/user/show/21807988-patricia-huynh">Patricia Huynh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer750264286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9627329415591850539"><b>5+++ Stars</b> it was so damn good.<br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>This book, this girl, the... the boys! I thought I was going to be torn between Zayne and Roth, even though I was a big Prince of Hell fan going in. I will admit I did like Zayne a lot more than I did previously because I am a girl, but I'm voting Roth all the way. And let's be real, if Bambi is going to be with Layla there should be Roth too.<br/><br/>SCT was a gem. JLA has a wicked sense of writing, characters and plot twists. The world building is phenomena</span></span>
  <span id="freeText9627329415591850539" style="display:none"><b>5+++ Stars</b> it was so damn good.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>This book, this girl, the... the boys! I thought I was going to be torn between Zayne and Roth, even though I was a big Prince of Hell fan going in. I will admit I did like Zayne a lot more than I did previously because I am a girl, but I'm voting Roth all the way. And let's be real, if Bambi is going to be with Layla there should be Roth too.<br><br>SCT was a gem. JLA has a wicked sense of writing, characters and plot twists. The world building is phenomenal. The tension and relationships between characters is palpable and well played.<br><br>Anyway, how can you overlook everything that Roth does? The sacrifices he made for Laya? For Zayne? This quote!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><i>"Can you hear me? I want you to know something," he said, his voice hoarse and thick and sounding so far away, but full of urgency. "I love you, Layla. Do you hear me? I've loved you since the first moment I heard your voice and I will continue to love you. No matter what. I love you."</i><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>But boy, some of those scenes...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414805606ra/11695560.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Phew. HOT!<br>Review on Every Last Breath:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/750264298?book_show_action=true&amp;page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br>---<br>So let me tell you how UPSET I was at the end of WHK. After Roth was gone I was just a mess...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394116034ra/8810305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then, it turns out my man is BACK! &lt;3 And I thought, "Oh..." too afraid to scream just yet.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394116034ra/8810306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, any good that did me. SO HELL YEAH ROTH'S BACK! &lt;33<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394115971ra/8810301.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>.... But, WTF that release date is going to blow.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394116034ra/8810307.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1346537925" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5792205435246177719">I have really mixed feelings about this book. I love Roth and Layla together and their scenes were the best part. I was absoulutly bored with Zayn and Layla. Roth is just perfect and was the only character who didn't annoy me at all. <br/>I loved the beginning and I thought it's getting even better than the first book. Than something happend and it got so boring. I was annoyed with all the characters ( except Roth )and basically rolled my eyes the hole time . There was no action and it was all about </span>
  <span id="freeText5792205435246177719" style="display:none">I have really mixed feelings about this book. I love Roth and Layla together and their scenes were the best part. I was absoulutly bored with Zayn and Layla. Roth is just perfect and was the only character who didn't annoy me at all. <br />I loved the beginning and I thought it's getting even better than the first book. Than something happend and it got so boring. I was annoyed with all the characters ( except Roth )and basically rolled my eyes the hole time . There was no action and it was all about this very complicated love triangle. I just couldn't force myself to sit and read about Zayn and Roth fighting over Layla. Zayn was too annoying and protective . It really bothered me that Layla would just let him order her around and treat her like she's a five year old who can't defend her self and will get hurt and die if she would be left alone. She was a half Warden and half demon so it's just didn't make sense why everyone (icluding her) thought she needs protection all the time. Warden's rules about women really made me angry which caused my huge hatred towards them (although they are the good guys) . It just didn't make any sense. Why would they stay home and gave birth to kids and be protected when they could also shift and have superpowers??? Very confused (and angry). The explenation is that they supposedly had to be protected so Wardens could continiue with their bloodline or something like that. It just doesen't make any sense. They could've anlist make decisions .<br />Also I was relly dissapointed with lack of action through the middle of the book. Everything was about their love triangle and nothing about the fantasy aspect of book . It was just thrown here and there to make some plot twists while Layla is hooking up with either Zayn or Roth. At some point I even stoped paing attention to anything about Lilin. But the book got really better towards the end and I really loved it later. There was more action and more Roth . I really like how things developed later . Also there is huge plot twist at the end although I kind of predicted it way before. I love this book ( despite it's flaws, that I choose to ignore )and I love the world and characters in it. I can't wait to read third part and see what happens at the end. Team Roth and Layla till the end. </span>

<div id="review_1438735810" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1438735810" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48100672-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602456592p2/48100672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1438735810?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/48100672-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48100672-amanda?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1438735810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9047267085376229378">I felt so many emotions with this book it was unreal, first I was team Roth then I was team Zayne then I was back to being team Roth my head felt like it was going to spin off! I really did not expect anything that was happening, I know some of you guys are like "oh god the usual YA cheese" because there is so much about the romances in this series I LOVE IT!! I WANT TO EAT ALL THE CHEESE!!!!!! I'm a sucker for a love story that has some wacky put into it and Jennifer L. Armentrout is just the w</span>
  <span id="freeText9047267085376229378" style="display:none">I felt so many emotions with this book it was unreal, first I was team Roth then I was team Zayne then I was back to being team Roth my head felt like it was going to spin off! I really did not expect anything that was happening, I know some of you guys are like "oh god the usual YA cheese" because there is so much about the romances in this series I LOVE IT!! I WANT TO EAT ALL THE CHEESE!!!!!! I'm a sucker for a love story that has some wacky put into it and Jennifer L. Armentrout is just the woman for the job.<br /><br />The story follows on from Layla's complete heartbreak after what Roth did for her, the girl was in serious shutdown mode. Again Zayne was there to pick all the pieces up and put them together again, but Roth returns and he ain't as loving as he was before but he's here to kick some serious ass with everything that's going on. During all this Layla loses her ability to see auras and things start to change for her, she is able to do more unexpected things shall we say. I really did feel for Sam &amp; Stacey I was total rooting for them the whole way... Also, if you aren't a fan of a big messy love triangle you should stay away from this one cause there is a lot of it!<br /><br />I love a strong character that you can picture in your mind and know exactly what they would look like and Armentrout makes it easy for you to do this. I love how she makes strong female characters too (Katy from the Lux series is my favourite leading lady.. EVER) but ole Layla isn't doing too bad either. Yeah, she can be a little pain in the ass but can you mind being a teenager for those around my age+? Your hormones were all over the place you didn't know if you were coming or going and trying to easily make your mind up about something... not happening! Then you had curfews, parents telling you what you can and cannot do and if you were like me sometimes you would stray from the righteous path that your parents were trying to lead you down but that's what being a teen is, and then came boys... the forbidden fruit! and Layla has a lovely pear right there! (See what a did... pear? Pair haha ok enough.)<br /><br />One thing I have noticed about this series was how overused some phrases were, then retelling of parts of the book sometimes it felt repetitive like it was trying to fill some parts? I don't know I noticed it slightly in the Lux series as well... but I still love both series I'm not going to lie! Once again I shut one book and went straight for the other.<br /><br />Please check my blog out and leave yours <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amandaminnockx.tumblr.com/">http://amandaminnockx.tumblr.com/</a> thanks :).<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“The loss of innocence refers to carnal sin and it's not like you have to do the deed to experience the pleasure of sin. Correct?!..<br /><br />Cayman dipped his chin.<br /><br />'In other words, all she needed to do was to have an orgasm..And most likely not by herself.'<br />..Someone kill me now!<br />..'Well.' Roth drew the word out.'This is awkward.'<br />I slowly lowered my hands.'You think?”</i>
</b><br /></span>

<div id="review_1146120272" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146120272" />
    <a title="Cody" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35007929-cody"><img alt="Cody" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415626292p2/35007929.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146120272?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cody" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cody" href="/user/show/35007929-cody">Cody</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146120272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer26358656059887405"><b>I loved reading this again!</b><br/><br/>Stone Cold Touch carries on from White Hot Kiss with Layla trying to come to terms with how different she is from her family and her life without Roth.<s>WHY?!</s><br/><br/>Layla becomes depressed, she misses Roth and worries constantly about his state in hell while Zayne tries his best to console her. <b>BUT</b> Roth is back! YESSSSS, and with that arrival it’s brings all kinds of feels and drama which he is famous for and at the most inappropriate of times! ;)<br/><br/>Zayne spends more time with Lay</span>
  <span id="freeText26358656059887405" style="display:none"><b>I loved reading this again!</b><br><br>Stone Cold Touch carries on from White Hot Kiss with Layla trying to come to terms with how different she is from her family and her life without Roth.<s>WHY?!</s><br><br>Layla becomes depressed, she misses Roth and worries constantly about his state in hell while Zayne tries his best to console her. <b>BUT</b> Roth is back! YESSSSS, and with that arrival it’s brings all kinds of feels and drama which he is famous for and at the most inappropriate of times! ;)<br><br>Zayne spends more time with Layla and finally admits how he feels... Enter the dangerous love triangle. For those who hate love triangles, this one was sort of necessary as JLA allowed the reader to decide who Layla would end up with. So as we were treated with lots of gorgeous moments of Roth in White Hot Kiss, Stone Cold Touch focused more on Zayne. Roth lovers fear not, you still get some hot scenes with the Crown Prince of Hell!<br><br>This is JLA hottest series yet and my god I fell for it hook, line and sinker. Yes it’s cheesy in parts but you eat it all up in its goodness with a racing heart. This isn’t your typical love triangle because Layla obviously can’t touch one of them and there is no frontrunner like Aiden in the Covenant Series. In White Hot Kiss it was all about Roth obviously and I hoped it would stay that way but this is Zayne’s book and dammit he’s so sweet and kind <s>argh</s>.<br><br>So am sure you all know that the voting is over but you guys better have voted for Roth! Seriously he’s just the perfect bad/good boy and he’s clearly the better match for Layla andddd he was there for her when Zayne wasn’t. Plus Roth just makes the book so much more entertaining with his snark!<br><br>I’m so excited for the final book and to find out who she finally ends up. JLA writing really did have a way of making me love Zayne even though I hate him! This series is my favourite of her work, it really brings out such strong emotions and I thoroughly enjoyed reading it a second time.<br><br>The writing is gorgeous, the characters are epic and the romance is to die for. So if you haven’t heard of this series seriously you need to read it now plus it’s HAWWWWT. The blurb says 'wickedly hot demon prince' and trust me that's exactly what you get &lt;3<br><br><b>
  <i>“I want you so badly it’s like hunger that gnaws at me endlessly. It doesn’t go away.”</i>

<div id="review_1684515064" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1684515064" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1684515064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2447688180004107821"><i>Stone Cold Touch</i> is the second book in <i>The Dark Elements</i> series and did slightly suffer from second book syndrome. It lacked the flare that the first book did and led me into a boredom on several accounts. This could be because I don't like Zayne, this could be because it was just a major info dumps, but I just didn't enjoy it too much. Character development was also non-existent. The romance was the main forefront, the plot taking the backseat in several circumstances. <br/><br/><u>
  <i>Characters</i>
</u><br/><b>Layla</b> was b</span>
  <span id="freeText2447688180004107821" style="display:none"><i>Stone Cold Touch</i> is the second book in <i>The Dark Elements</i> series and did slightly suffer from second book syndrome. It lacked the flare that the first book did and led me into a boredom on several accounts. This could be because I don't like Zayne, this could be because it was just a major info dumps, but I just didn't enjoy it too much. Character development was also non-existent. The romance was the main forefront, the plot taking the backseat in several circumstances. <br /><br /><u>
  <i>Characters</i>
</u><br /><b>Layla</b> was better than the first book. She had a bit more of a backbone and stood up for herself. However, Layla was also boy obsessed and in the worst moments would find her making out with a boy to <i>forget what was going on</i>. She infuriated me, but it was nice to see her actually do something i.e. jump into a fight. <br /><br /><b>Roth</b> was again the best character. He actually did stuff that didn't benefit himself. He was trying to protect Layla or give Zayne a chance (around bickering with him). He protected Layla always, despite being the asshole he is. Though, I wouldn't say he was the biggest asshole overall because that title goes to the wardens. <br /><br /><b>Zayne</b> was just an egotistic asshole. That's all I've got. I just don't like him. He's judgey and makes me uncomfortable. He's also strangely sexist, not ever believing in Layla or saying she can't be involved in fights. I understand protective but his wording came across as oddly sexist. <br /><br /><u>
  <i>Plot</i>
</u><br />What plot? I mean, there was a plot when the love triangle wasn't taking over -- and it <b>was</b> interesting. I did guess the plot twist ending (so not a cliffhanger). <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sam was very obviously the one doing it, the personality change he underwent was too sporadic to not be a clue. I mean, he didn't even drop his fun facts. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><u>
  <i>Writing</i>
</u><br />The problems I had in the first book, like unrealistic dialogue, fixed themselves in this book. I was glad to not have to cringe at every other line. But, I did find myself cringing I really at Zayne's character. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sincerely wish that Layla had just taken his soul entirely. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Overall</i>
</u><br />It wasn't a bad book, but it wasn't a good book. It had its good moments and it's bad moments, which is why I have decided this book falls at a solid three stars in my opinion.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2447688180004107821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_634379868" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/634379868" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/634379868?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=don-t-be-fooled-by-the-cover">don-t-be-fooled-by-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=serious-cliffhanger">serious-cliffhanger</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer634379868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14239335125379965576"><b>
  <i>"I want you so badly it's like a hunger that gnaws at me endlessly. It doesn't go away." He dipped his head to the space between my neck and shoulder, inhaling deeply. "You have no fucking clue."<br/>"Then do something about it," I whispered.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Thank God. <i>Thank. Gooood.</i> I am not going to lie to you all. I have been soooo nervous these last few months about my relationship with JLA. I think it's because of her NA series. It just doesn't touch me the way you'd think it should, seeing as she's been my </span>
  <span id="freeText14239335125379965576" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"I want you so badly it's like a hunger that gnaws at me endlessly. It doesn't go away." He dipped his head to the space between my neck and shoulder, inhaling deeply. "You have no fucking clue."<br>"Then do something about it," I whispered.</i>
</b><br><br>Thank God. <i>Thank. Gooood.</i> I am not going to lie to you all. I have been soooo nervous these last few months about my relationship with JLA. I think it's because of her NA series. It just doesn't touch me the way you'd think it should, seeing as she's been my favorite author for a good two years or so. But, in the last year I've started to see and feel....some different feelings. I've seen changes in Armentrout's work. She's began to use repetitive phrasing occurring in each and every book she produces and anyone who knows me at all knows that is a <b>Hell NO</b> for me. And, I'll be honest, if it wasn't such childish phrasing it wouldn't bother me-at all. But, as it is, <i>Holy crap on a cracker</i> and <i>Holy alien babies</i> doesn't make me laugh like it once used to in her Lux and Covenant series. No, it makes me roll my eyes. <b>Hard.</b> But, as I said in my last JLA review in her NA series, I really do think her bread and butter is paranormal romance. I felt that was a bold statement and that maybe I was just <i>hoping</i> that was the case. But, here comes Roth and all my doubts were obliterated-<b>this was everything I've ever loved about JLA.</b> I knew it. I just <i>knew</i> it.<br><br><b>I wasn't thinking as I reached over and plucked the hamburger right out of his hand. Twisting at the waist, I threw the hamburger on the floor behind Roth as hard as I could. The satisfactory <i>splat</i> it made as ketchup and mayo splattered like a gruesome burger massacre brought a wide smile to my face.<br>Stacey let out a burst of shocked laughter.<br>Roth glanced down at the hamburger and then his gaze slowly tracked back to mine. His eyes were wide. "But I really wanted that hamburger."</b><br><br>I was in a sleepy haze allll weekend. I'm not guna lie. It was a struggle to read any and every page for whatever reason (Hey, it was a busy weekend!) so I was extremely nervous it would effect my overall feeling for the whole novel. This is partly true, but it was <b>so</b> good that I still came out thinking, 'Wow, 5 stars!!!' I missed some of the sexiness. I missed some of the peril. But nothing can beat peril peril peril peril peril and sexy scene sexy scene sexy scene and a badass twist near the end....it was one hot or action-packed thing after another and it became difficult <i>not</i> to see what was right in front of my face. One thing I do know is that when book three comes out, I will be doing a re-read....and I never do re-reads (hardly) before a new release for a series. It takes too long and makes me all flighty. Point being-this will be like a whole new book to me when I re-read it because I missed so much.<br><br><b>I almost rushed Roth right then and threw my arms around him, but a low growl rumbled from behind me. At first I thought it was Abbot's response, but when I realized it was coming from Zayne, I couldn't move.<br>Roth tilted his head to the side, watching me as a slow, roguish smile graced his lips. "Are you...seriously growling at me, Stony?"<br>"I'm about to do a lot more than growl."<br>He chuckled. "That's not very appreciative."</b><br><br>I will also admit another thing-<b>to those of you who loathe love triangles, pass this one up.</b> I've always thought Armentrout is very clear about who is going to be the final male in the end. It's <b>always</b> been easy to tell. But...I think she was approached by her marketing people for this one because what was once a landslide victory for my dark demon Roth is now a murky, convoluted mess of a Zayne and Roth banana split. Seriously. This is her first novel where (everyone is supposed to vote for which guy she ends up with) I have no clue if my guy will win. Like....really? Why, Jen?? Whhhhyyyyy? It was excellent, sure. But it was also clear that Layla is in love with two guys. I'm not going to lie, though, I think her feelings are stronger for Roth. I really do. Zayne has been someone she's loved since she met him. Roth is that fresh guy that swooped her up when Zayne didn't want anything to do with her....and I think that really impacted her. She just won't let him go....and I think Armentrout kinda did that on purpose-All of Zayne's scenes were super hot and sweet and I wouldn't DIE if she ended up with him because of all the nuts who would vote for him but I really and truly believe, that despite what JLA is saying on the voting page, she wants and believes she should be with Roth. It was like that in book one, and then it did a complete 360. And every word or phrase kinda hinted at how much Roth got under her skin and how he let her be herself. I loved that...and I think it was a true reflection on the author's feelings. The truth of what she wants came out in her writing.<br><br><b>Roth came back up the step, crowding me. As he dipped his head so that his mouth nearly brushed mine when he spoke, I refused to back away. "I know why you say that. I even understand it, Layla. I get it. I hurt you and deserve every single one of your lies."<br>I stilled as his warm breath danced over my lips.<br>"But there is so much you don't know or understand," he said, tilting his head so that his words brushed the lobe of my ear, sending a shiver down my neck. "So don't claim to know what I really want or what I would do to protect it."</b><br><br>I really have a soft spot for Layla. She's funny, loyal, determined. She's flawed and not altogether a goody-goody. I like her obsession with sweets (ie sugar cookie cookie-dough) because it helps her to satiate the urge she gets for soul-sucking lol. I love how that's her replacement. I like how she interacts with her friends and how she doesn't shy away from a battle. There are many things Layla is, including scared a lot of the time, but she's not a coward. I love it.<br><br><b>"Shut up, whore of Satan."<br>My mouth dropped open and my head was about to spin <i>Exorcist-</i>style. I stepped forward as Roth cracked his neck, signaling he was ready to end this little conversation. "Call me that one more time and I'll give you something to fear." I had no idea where those words came from because, even with Zayne's training, I wasn't really a fighter, and I wasn't a badass, but my lips curved into a cold, tight smile. "That's a promise."</b><br><br>So, I will stop here because as I said, the details are fuzzy as it is and I will be re-reading this anyway but I'll sum up a bit-The plot was super strong (for me) and there was a lot of love in this one. It wasn't the loving I wanted but we still got plenty of each guy. I liked the mystery behind who was reeking havoc on the school and wardens alike, even more I liked the way Armentrout channeled her evil side again (she hasn't been so evil since my fav books <i>Obsidian, Onyx,</i>and <i>Opal</i>) and let the blood and betrayal fly...and we know how I love that. I don't know, I just really love this series, and even more I love that it's a trilogy. 5 books is too many, three will sum this all up perfectly....and I can't wait to see who our part demon chooses....<b>you assholes better vote for Roth.</b> <br><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491628712i/22430034._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " href="/user/show/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict">bibliophile (Romance Addict) </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=step-bro_sis">step-bro_sis</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=made-me-cry-like-a-baby">made-me-cry-like-a-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=magic">magic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1353804713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1282932499709075886"><b>4.5 Layla Bug Stars!<br/><br/>“But Roth was like this little devil on my shoulder, urging me to be bad and to enjoy every freaking moment of it. Except he wasn’t a little devil. He was the Crown Prince of Hell.”<br/><br/><br/></b><br/><br/><b>Series:</b> This is the second book in the White Hot Kiss series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. It is written in Layla's POV.<br/><br/><b>Story:</b> This book complete what happened in White Hot Kiss. Roth disappeared, and Layla miss him a lot. She can't stop thinking about the way he disappeared and the only person who he</span>
  <span id="freeText1282932499709075886" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Layla Bug Stars!<br /><br />“But Roth was like this little devil on my shoulder, urging me to be bad and to enjoy every freaking moment of it. Except he wasn’t a little devil. He was the Crown Prince of Hell.”<br /><br /><br /></b><br /><br /><b>Series:</b> This is the second book in the White Hot Kiss series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. It is written in Layla's POV.<br /><br /><b>Story:</b> This book complete what happened in White Hot Kiss. Roth disappeared, and Layla miss him a lot. She can't stop thinking about the way he disappeared and the only person who helps her to get over Roth, is Zayne. The love triangle in this book made me mad, but I have to admit I still enjoyed the two guys presence in Layla's life. However, I AM ON TEAM ROTH!! Forever &amp; always!! <br /><br /><b>Characters:</b> Layla was fun to read through even though I wanted to punch her in the face sometimes. She whined &amp; didn't know her own feelings, so nobody should blame me. Yet I couldn't blame her since I liked both guys. Of course, Roth was a lot more tempting, but Zayne wasn't bad, and I had a hard time hating him in this book. <br /><br />At the same time, I hated Abbot. What kind of a father figure would do that to his supposed to be daughter? That was some pretty messed up thing to do. I really liked Dez, Danika, Jas, and Nicolai. I didn't know whether they started hating Layla or not, but we knew at the end who was on her side. <br /><br /><b>Ending:</b> CLIFFHANGER!!! Whyyyyyyy???<br /><br /><b>Why not 5 Stars?</b><br /><br />First, the plot twist was easy to predict. I always loved the way Jennifer's books were unpredictable. This was different though which made me rate it lesser than it was supposed to be. I wasn't surprised by the end, but I guess the surprising factor happened at other times. <br /><br />I am on team Roth, and in this book, he was barely there. I was waiting for him to reappear, but Layla got deeper into her own wishful thinking with Zayne. Anyways, I honestly did like Zyane's parts, but Roth was a lot better for me. <br /><br /><b>Writing:</b> Jennifer L. Armentrout's writing is amazing. I guess this is one of the reasons why I never felt bored even though nothing big happened in this book. I liked it though.<br /><br />I recommend this series to Paranormal/romance readers!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1282932499709075886" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3655874915" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3655874915" />
    <a title="krista ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72478075-krista"><img alt="krista ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604762085p2/72478075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3655874915?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="krista ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="krista ☽" href="/user/show/72478075-krista">krista ☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781335009203" href="/book/show/42246378-stone-cold-touch">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3655874915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13048462071973479454"><b>“I love you Layla. Do you hear me? I've loved you since the first moment I heard your voice and I will continue to love you. No matter what. I love you.” </b>- Roth , Damn yes you do i knew it ! <br/><b> “Maddox hissed. “You think you’re cute?”<br/>“Nah, I think I’m sexy.” The smirk spread, but it didn’t reach his cool ocher eyes. “And I also think I’m hilarious.” </b> - Roth again , what a big suprise hehe. He is hillarious period. <br/><br/><b> I reccoment Jennifer her books for people who like very fast urban fantasy entertai</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13048462071973479454" style="display:none"><b>“I love you Layla. Do you hear me? I've loved you since the first moment I heard your voice and I will continue to love you. No matter what. I love you.” </b>- Roth , Damn yes you do i knew it ! <br /><b> “Maddox hissed. “You think you’re cute?”<br />“Nah, I think I’m sexy.” The smirk spread, but it didn’t reach his cool ocher eyes. “And I also think I’m hilarious.” </b> - Roth again , what a big suprise hehe. He is hillarious period. <br /><br /><b> I reccoment Jennifer her books for people who like very fast urban fantasy entertaining books with lots of angst and romance and twistst and turns. But who doesnt mind tropes because it does have a lot of tropes. Bad guy and goodgirl love story , sassy bad guy love intrest , main charracters with special powers but i feel like when Jennifer does these tropes they are done very well and i personally do love it and dont mind the tropes </b> <br /><br /><b> Stone cold touch </b> is the second book in the Dark elements triology by Jennifer l. Armentrout. I really loved the first book <b> White hot kiss </b> it was a great book and i also really enjoyed and loved this one &lt;3 <br /><b>So what did i like about this book ?</b><br />Jennifer l. Armentrout just has a way with storys and then especially in making them so freaking addictive. Every book i have readed by her so far was a addictive keeping my up allnight and forgetting about sleep kinda book. And those books are the <b> best </b> books &lt;3 Like the first book this book was full of action and urban fantasy worldbuilding stuff and urban fantasy plot with a lot of twistst even more then in the first book wich i loved because i am a sucker for twistst that get me like whoa whate the hell!? The charracters are all fun and funny and there is again a lot of banter in this book but also somuch angst , like somuch angst is in this book again even more then in the first one. and i love angst hehe. So yes this book was really good and it is a fast read but the thing with jennifer l. armentrout her books is that they are fast and have a fast action paced plot but they still are deep and they dont lose their depht as amny super fast paced books do. The charracters are still well developt and struggle with things. + a lot of steamy scenes in the romance department + also the thing i love the most about this book ROTH ROTH ROTh oh and ROTh oh aaaaaand ROTH!!!! and bambi , bambi , bambi , bambi and bambi. i love my bambie and i love my roth. Oh and the kittens tatoes. <br /><br />This book starts of like 2 weeks after white hot kiss ended. Layla is grieving because of Roth and struggels a lot with that. Zayne is there for her wich is really nice of him. And then we have strange things happening to people that Layla had been in contact with but why are these things happening? and suddenly Roth is back and he is like no Layla i never felt anything from you but we have a problem so i am back because the soul sucking Lillin is back. and then there the plot goes :) Also romance is again a big point in this one , in the first book i loved Roth and Layla and i still do. they are my ship i love them somuch. But in this book we sort of have a kinda love triangle going on because Layla also grows close to Zayne in a different kind of way because he admits his feelings and then we have a lot of inner conflict in Layla her head. I didnt struggle because i am team Roth all the way. Normally i hate love triangles with a passion , in this book i did not mind it that much. I was team Roth all the way so i was like no Zayne and Layla just no but it wasnt really annoying and stupidly done like the love triangle is understandable and i do love the relationship between Layla and Zayne and it is something special but it isnt it in my believe. they are just more brother and sister and very close friends. <br /><br />I liked Layla the main protagonist in this book , she struggels a lot and that felt really real like not only her struggels with the love triangle but the stuff about i dont bellong and i dont feel like i can by myself anywhere , where can i be myself , wich people accept me , her lonelyness. + she is brave and kind and funny. I enjoy her quite a lot as a main charracter. I love Roth obv. And i do like Zayne but it keeps being weird because i know him from the habringer books. He is really sweet tho but he has to stop listening to his goddamn father. <br /><br /><b> a little more about Roth and Layla and Roth cause i need to fangurl </b> <br />Roth and Layla , i ship them so hard. Roth cares about Layla and even tho he denies it the entire book i knew that it wasnt true. and then we have the scenes at the ending , baby it is going to be okay ugh , he tells Layla he loves her somuch and i knew it. Those scenes ugh &lt;3 I also feel like Layla can be her true self with Roth more then with Zayne and that fits better , it is less complicated in a way and Roth wants to protect Layla but lets her do her own thing and lets her fight and doesnt want to put her in a little glass house, zayne kinda does. [This is like tamlin vs Rhys kinda?] And their banter is so fun &lt;3 they just fitt sowell , and those steamy scenes DAMN YES!!! i live for their steamy scenes. And roth is such an amazing sassy charracter , i love this guy and i love Bambi. <br /><br />Great sequel , i really enjoyed myself reading this and i flew trough it. Its just a really entertaining book. I do think i liked the first one a little more , cant wait for the final book because OMG that huge plottwist at the end i was shoooooked omg. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13048462071973479454" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer11060420005043654479"><b>HOLY MOTHER OF PLOT TWISTS</b><br/><br/>To be honest, I prefered the first book... I just felt like the main focus of this one was the love triangle between Layla, hot ass Upper Level demon Roth and sweetheart Warden Zayne. And, like I said before, I strongly dislike love triangles. But in general the book was pretty great, like every book written by our dear Jennifer L. Armentrout, I mostly enjoyed every chapter. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I FUCKING KNEW THERE WAS SOMETHING WRONG ABOUT NEW SAM BUT I DIDN'T EXPECT SUCH </span></span>
